if (!is_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd') != '3e3fb181982d071063b3aa76b21d9e1c3e080a85') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd') !== '3e3fb181982d071063b3aa76b21d9e1c3e080a85') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd') !== '9c8378320b8951e656f3002d9faa9e948206a729') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd') !== '3e3fb181982d071063b3aa76b21d9e1c3e080a85') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '2283561d0c889f351e89ea3b7d079ccdf2cbbff2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2283561d0c889f351e89ea3b7d079ccdf2cbbff2') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'a9cc981e1c42c62188a47fc8fde80ff0cf403f9e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2283561d0c889f351e89ea3b7d079ccdf2cbbff2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
